### Development Step 1: Identify Postmaster General Who Launched First Scheduled Turnpike Road Postal Delivery System

**Description**: Research the history of postal systems to identify the person who served as Postmaster General and introduced a postal system that first implemented scheduled delivery times and operated on turnpike roads. Focus on early postal system developments, particularly in countries known for pioneering organized mail delivery systems such as Britain, France, or early American postal services. Search for keywords including 'first scheduled postal delivery', 'turnpike road postal system', 'Postmaster General scheduled delivery times', and 'early postal system turnpike roads'.

**Use Cases**:
- Archival digitization and metadata tagging of 18th-century mail coach schedules for museum collections
- GIS-based analysis of historic turnpike road mail routes for urban planners optimizing modern transport corridors
- Development of interactive educational modules on John Palmer’s postal reforms for secondary history curricula
- Automated extraction of postal regulation changes from 18th-century documents for legal historians studying pre-modern communication laws
- Philatelic database enhancement with cataloged mail coach route data for stamp collecting societies
- AI-driven sentiment and content analysis on archival correspondence delivered via scheduled mail coaches for digital humanities scholars
- Logistic network simulation using historical postal schedules to model early transport efficiency in supply chain courses
- Cultural tourism planning using re-creations of mail coach journeys and schedules for heritage travel agencies

```
import os
import requests
import json
from datetime import datetime

print("Researching the history of postal systems to identify the Postmaster General who introduced scheduled delivery times on turnpike roads...")

# Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist
if not os.path.exists('workspace'):
os.makedirs('workspace')

def get_serpapi_key():
"""Get SerpAPI key from environment variables"""
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")
if api_key is None:
print("Warning: SERPAPI_API_KEY not found in environment variables")
print("Will proceed with hardcoded historical research approach")
return api_key

def search_google(query, max_results=10):
"""Search Google using SerpAPI for postal system history"""
api_key = get_serpapi_key()
if not api_key:
return None

params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": max_results,
}

try:
print(f"Searching Google for: {query}")
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()
if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} search results")
return results["organic_results"]
else:
print(f"No results found for '{query}'")
return []
else:
print(f"Search API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}")
return None
except Exception as e:
print(f"Error during search: {str(e)}")
return None

def get_page_content(url):
"""Fetch content from a URL with proper headers"""
headers = {
'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36'
}

try:
print(f"Fetching content from: {url}")
response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=30)
response.raise_for_status()
print(f"Successfully fetched content from: {url}")
return response.text
except Exception as e:
print(f"Error fetching {url}: {str(e)}")
return None

def research_postal_history():
"""Research postal system history focusing on scheduled delivery and turnpike roads"""
print("\nStarting comprehensive research on postal system history...")

# Define search queries for different aspects of postal history
search_queries = [
"first scheduled postal delivery turnpike roads Postmaster General",
"early postal system scheduled delivery times Britain France America",
"turnpike road postal system history Postmaster General",
"Palmer mail coach system Britain scheduled delivery",
"Benjamin Franklin Postmaster General scheduled postal delivery",
"John Palmer postal reform Britain turnpike roads 1784"
]

all_search_results = []

# Perform searches
for query in search_queries:
results = search_google(query, max_results=5)
if results:
all_search_results.extend(results)
# Add a small delay between searches
import time
time.sleep(1)

# Save search results
search_results_file = "workspace/postal_history_search_results.json"
with open(search_results_file, 'w') as f:
json.dump({
"timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
"queries": search_queries,
"total_results": len(all_search_results),
"results": all_search_results
}, f, indent=2)

print(f"\nSaved {len(all_search_results)} search results to {search_results_file}")

# Analyze search results for key information
key_findings = []

for result in all_search_results:
title = result.get('title', '')
snippet = result.get('snippet', '')
link = result.get('link', '')

# Look for key terms related to our research
key_terms = ['palmer', 'mail coach', 'turnpike', 'scheduled', 'postmaster general',
'benjamin franklin', '1784', 'postal reform', 'delivery times']

found_terms = [term for term in key_terms if term.lower() in (title + ' ' + snippet).lower()]

if found_terms:
key_findings.append({
'title': title,
'snippet': snippet,
'link': link,
'relevant_terms': found_terms
})

print(f"\nFound {len(key_findings)} results with relevant terms")

# Display key findings
for i, finding in enumerate(key_findings[:10]): # Show top 10
print(f"\n--- Finding {i+1} ---")
print(f"Title: {finding['title']}")
print(f"Snippet: {finding['snippet']}")
print(f"Relevant terms: {', '.join(finding['relevant_terms'])}")
print(f"Link: {finding['link']}")

return key_findings

- Automating literature searches and primary‐source collection for a historian writing a peer-reviewed journal article on turnpike-based postal reforms in Britain and early America
- Advising modern postal operators on route scheduling improvements by extracting historical performance metrics (e.g., London-Bath delivery times) as case studies in a logistics consultancy white paper
- Powering a documentary production’s research pipeline to retrieve and verify web content on Benjamin Franklin’s and John Palmer’s postal innovations for on-screen graphics and narration scripts

import os
import requests
import json
from datetime import datetime

print("Researching the history of postal systems to identify the Postmaster General who introduced scheduled delivery times on turnpike roads...")

# Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist
if not os.path.exists('workspace'):
os.makedirs('workspace')

# ============================================================================
# FUNCTION DEFINITIONS - All functions defined first before execution
# ============================================================================

def get_serpapi_key():
"""Get SerpAPI key from environment variables"""
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")
if api_key is None:
print("Warning: SERPAPI_API_KEY not found in environment variables")
print("Will proceed with hardcoded historical research approach")
return api_key

def search_google(query, max_results=10):
"""Search Google using SerpAPI for postal system history"""
api_key = get_serpapi_key()
if not api_key:
print(f"Skipping Google search for '{query}' - no API key available")
return None

params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": max_results,
}

try:
print(f"Searching Google for: {query}")
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()
if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} search results")
return results["organic_results"]
else:
print(f"No results found for '{query}'")
return []
else:
print(f"Search API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}")
return None
except Exception as e:
print(f"Error during search: {str(e)}")
return None

def get_page_content(url):
"""Fetch content from a URL with proper headers"""
headers = {
'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36'
}

try:
print(f"Fetching content from: {url}")
response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=30)
response.raise_for_status()
print(f"Successfully fetched content from: {url}")
return response.text
except Exception as e:
print(f"Error fetching {url}: {str(e)}")
return None

def research_postal_history():
"""Research postal system history focusing on scheduled delivery and turnpike roads"""
print("\nStarting comprehensive research on postal system history...")

# Define search queries for different aspects of postal history
search_queries = [
"John Palmer mail coach system 1784 turnpike scheduled delivery",
"first scheduled postal delivery turnpike roads Postmaster General",
"Benjamin Franklin Postmaster General scheduled postal delivery turnpikes",
"Palmer mail coach system Britain scheduled delivery turnpike roads",
"early postal system scheduled delivery times Britain France America",
"Lord Sandwich Postmaster General Palmer mail coach turnpike"
]

all_search_results = []

# Perform searches if API key is available
for query in search_queries:
results = search_google(query, max_results=5)
if results:
all_search_results.extend(results)
elif results is not None: # Empty results but API worked
print(f"No results found for: {query}")
# Add a small delay between searches
import time
time.sleep(1)

# Save search results
search_results_file = "workspace/postal_history_search_results.json"
with open(search_results_file, 'w') as f:
json.dump({
"timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
"queries": search_queries,
"total_results": len(all_search_results),
"results": all_search_results
}, f, indent=2)

print(f"\nSaved {len(all_search_results)} search results to {search_results_file}")

# Analyze search results for key information
key_findings = []

for result in all_search_results:
title = result.get('title', '')
snippet = result.get('snippet', '')
link = result.get('link', '')

# Look for key terms related to our research
key_terms = ['palmer', 'mail coach', 'turnpike', 'scheduled', 'postmaster general',
'benjamin franklin', '1784', 'postal reform', 'delivery times', 'sandwich']

found_terms = [term for term in key_terms if term.lower() in (title + ' ' + snippet).lower()]

if found_terms:
key_findings.append({
'title': title,
'snippet': snippet,
'link': link,
'relevant_terms': found_terms
})

print(f"\nFound {len(key_findings)} results with relevant terms")

# Display key findings
for i, finding in enumerate(key_findings[:10]): # Show top 10
print(f"\n--- Finding {i+1} ---")
print(f"Title: {finding['title']}")
print(f"Snippet: {finding['snippet']}")
print(f"Relevant terms: {', '.join(finding['relevant_terms'])}")
print(f"Link: {finding['link']}")

return key_findings

import os import requests import json from datetime import datetime print("Researching Indiana's first governor and the Interstate 65 section named in their honor...") # Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist if not os.path.exists('workspace'): os.makedirs('workspace') print("\nStep 1: Identifying Indiana's first governor...") # Historical data about Indiana's first governor indiana_governor_data = { "first_governor": { "name": "Jonathan Jennings", "role": "First Governor of Indiana", "term": "1816-1822", "birth_year": 1784, "death_year": 1834, "birthplace": "Hunterdon County, New Jersey", "significance": "Led Indiana to statehood and served as its first governor", "key_achievements": [ "Moved to Indiana Territory in 1806", "Served as Indiana's delegate to Congress (1809-1816)", "Instrumental in Indiana achieving statehood on December 11, 1816", "Elected as Indiana's first governor in 1816", "Served two terms as governor (1816-1822)", "Later served in U.S. House of Representatives (1822-1831)", "Died in 1834 in Charlestown, Indiana" ] }, "statehood_context": { "date": "December 11, 1816", "order": "19th state to join the Union", "significance": "Jonathan Jennings was key figure in statehood process" } } print(f"Indiana's first governor: {indiana_governor_data['first_governor']['name']}") print(f"Term: {indiana_governor_data['first_governor']['term']}") print(f"Role in statehood: {indiana_governor_data['first_governor']['significance']}") print("\nStep 2: Searching for information about I-65 section named after Jonathan Jennings...") # Check for API key api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key: print("SerpAPI key found - attempting searches...") else: print("No SerpAPI key available - will use historical research approach") # Define search queries for I-65 Jonathan Jennings research search_queries = [ "Jonathan Jennings Interstate 65 Indiana named section", "I-65 Jonathan Jennings highway designation Indiana legislature", "23.6 mile Interstate 65 Indiana governor named", "Indiana highway naming resolution Jonathan Jennings I-65", "Interstate 65 Indiana Jonathan Jennings legislative resolution", "I-65 section named after Indiana first governor" ] all_search_results = [] # Perform searches if API key is available if api_key: for query in search_queries: try: print(f"\nSearching: {query}") params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "num": 5 } response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=20) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): all_search_results.extend(results["organic_results"]) print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results") else: print("No results found") else: print(f"Search failed with status {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"Search error: {str(e)}") # Small delay between searches import time time.sleep(1) print(f"\nTotal search results collected: {len(all_search_results)}") else: print("Skipping web searches - no API key available") # Save search results search_results_file = "workspace/jennings_i65_search_results.json" with open(search_results_file, 'w') as f: json.dump({ "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(), "governor_identified": "Jonathan Jennings", "search_queries": search_queries, "total_results": len(all_search_results), "results": all_search_results }, f, indent=2) print(f"\nSearch results saved to {search_results_file}") print("\nStep 3: Analyzing search results for I-65 highway information...") # Analyze search results for relevant information highway_findings = { "relevant_results": [], "potential_dates": [], "legislative_references": [], "highway_details": [] } for result in all_search_results: title = result.get('title', '') snippet = result.get('snippet', '') link = result.get('link', '') combined_text = (title + ' ' + snippet).lower() # Look for key terms key_terms = ['interstate 65', 'i-65', 'jennings', 'highway', 'resolution', 'legislature', '23.6', 'mile', 'section', 'named', 'designated'] found_terms = [term for term in key_terms if term in combined_text] if len(found_terms) >= 3: # Must have at least 3 relevant terms highway_findings['relevant_results'].append({ 'title': title, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': link, 'found_terms': found_terms }) # Look for years/dates import re years = re.findall(r'\b(19|20)\d{2}\b', combined_text) highway_findings['potential_dates'].extend(years) # Look for legislative terms if any(term in combined_text for term in ['resolution', 'legislature', 'passed', 'designated']): highway_findings['legislative_references'].append({ 'title': title, 'snippet': snippet, 'text_excerpt': combined_text[:200] + '...' if len(combined_text) > 200 else combined_text }) print(f"Found {len(highway_findings['relevant_results'])} highly relevant results") print(f"Found {len(highway_findings['legislative_references'])} results with legislative terms") print(f"Potential dates mentioned: {sorted(set(highway_findings['potential_dates']))}") # Display relevant findings if highway_findings['relevant_results']: print("\nMost relevant search results:") for i, result in enumerate(highway_findings['relevant_results'][:5], 1): print(f"\n--- Result {i} ---") print(f"Title: {result['title']}") print(f"Snippet: {result['snippet']}") print(f"Relevant terms: {', '.join(result['found_terms'])}") print(f"Link: {result['link']}") else: print("\nNo highly relevant results found in initial search.") print("This may require more specific search terms or different approaches.") if highway_findings['legislative_references']: print("\nResults mentioning legislative action:") for i, ref in enumerate(highway_findings['legislative_references'][:3], 1): print(f"\n--- Legislative Reference {i} ---") print(f"Title: {ref['title']}") print(f"Snippet: {ref['snippet']}") print("\nStep 4: Compiling comprehensive analysis...") # import os import requests import json from datetime import datetime print("Researching Indiana's first governor and the Interstate 65 section named in their honor...") # Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist if not os.path.exists('workspace'): os.makedirs('workspace') print("\nStep 1: Identifying Indiana's first governor...") # Historical data about Indiana's first governor indiana_governor_data = { "first_governor": { "name": "Jonathan Jennings", "role": "First Governor of Indiana", "term": "1816-1822", "birth_year": 1784, "death_year": 1834, "birthplace": "Hunterdon County, New Jersey", "significance": "Led Indiana to statehood and served as its first governor", "key_achievements": [ "Moved to Indiana Territory in 1806", "Served as Indiana's delegate to Congress (1809-1816)", "Instrumental in Indiana achieving statehood on December 11, 1816", "Elected as Indiana's first governor in 1816", "Served two terms as governor (1816-1822)", "Later served in U.S. House of Representatives (1822-1831)", "Died in 1834 in Charlestown, Indiana" ] }, "statehood_context": { "date": "December 11, 1816", "order": "19th state to join the Union", "significance": "Jonathan Jennings was key figure in statehood process" } } print(f"Indiana's first governor: {indiana_governor_data['first_governor']['name']}") print(f"Term: {indiana_governor_data['first_governor']['term']}") print(f"Role in statehood: {indiana_governor_data['first_governor']['significance']}") print("\nStep 2: Searching for information about I-65 section named after Jonathan Jennings...") # Check for API key api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key: print("SerpAPI key found - attempting searches...") else: print("No SerpAPI key available - will use historical research approach") # Define search queries for I-65 Jonathan Jennings research search_queries = [ "Jonathan Jennings Interstate 65 Indiana named section", "I-65 Jonathan Jennings highway designation Indiana legislature", "23.6 mile Interstate 65 Indiana governor named", "Indiana highway naming resolution Jonathan Jennings I-65", "Interstate 65 Indiana Jonathan Jennings legislative resolution", "I-65 section named after Indiana first governor" ] all_search_results = [] # Perform searches if API key is available if api_key: for query in search_queries: try: print(f"\nSearching: {query}") params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "num": 5 } response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=20) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): all_search_results.extend(results["organic_results"]) print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results") else: print("No results found") else: print(f"Search failed with status {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"Search error: {str(e)}") # Small delay between searches import time time.sleep(1) print(f"\nTotal search results collected: {len(all_search_results)}") else: print("Skipping web searches - no API key available") # Save search results search_results_file = "workspace/jennings_i65_search_results.json" with open(search_results_file, 'w') as f: json.dump({ "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(), "governor_identified": "Jonathan Jennings", "search_queries": search_queries, "total_results": len(all_search_results), "results": all_search_results }, f, indent=2) print(f"\nSearch results saved to {search_results_file}") print("\nStep 3: Analyzing search results for I-65 highway information...") # Analyze search results for relevant information highway_findings = { "relevant_results": [], "potential_dates": [], "legislative_references": [], "highway_details": [] } for result in all_search_results: title = result.get('title', '') snippet = result.get('snippet', '') link = result.get('link', '') combined_text = (title + ' ' + snippet).lower() # Look for key terms key_terms = ['interstate 65', 'i-65', 'jennings', 'highway', 'resolution', 'legislature', '23.6', 'mile', 'section', 'named', 'designated'] found_terms = [term for term in key_terms if term in combined_text] if len(found_terms) >= 3: # Must have at least 3 relevant terms highway_findings['relevant_results'].append({ 'title': title, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': link, 'found_terms': found_terms }) # Look for years/dates import re years = re.findall(r'\b(19|20)\d{2}\b', combined_text) highway_findings['potential_dates'].extend(years) # Look for legislative terms if any(term in combined_text for term in ['resolution', 'legislature', 'passed', 'designated']): highway_findings['legislative_references'].append({ 'title': title, 'snippet': snippet, 'text_excerpt': combined_text[:200] + '...' if len(combined_text) > 200 else combined_text }) print(f"Found {len(highway_findings['relevant_results'])} highly relevant results") print(f"Found {len(highway_findings['legislative_references'])} results with legislative terms") print(f"Potential dates mentioned: {sorted(set(highway_findings['potential_dates']))}") # Display relevant findings if highway_findings['relevant_results']: print("\nMost relevant search results:") for i, result in enumerate(highway_findings['relevant_results'][:5], 1): print(f"\n--- Result {i} ---") print(f"Title: {result['title']}") print(f"Snippet: {result['snippet']}") print(f"Relevant terms: {', '.join(result['found_terms'])}") print(f"Link: {result['link']}") else: print("\nNo highly relevant results found in initial search.") print("This may require more specific search terms or different approaches.") if highway_findings['legislative_references']: print("\nResults mentioning legislative action:") for i, ref in enumerate(highway_findings['legislative_references'][:3], 1): print(f"\n--- Legislative Reference {i} ---") print(f"Title: {ref['title']}") print(f"Snippet: {ref['snippet']}") print("\nStep 4: Compiling comprehensive analysis...") # Create comprehensive analysis comprehensive_analysis = { "research_question": "When did Indiana legislature pass resolution to name 23.6-mile I-65 section after Jonathan Jennings?", "governor_identification": { "name": "Jonathan Jennings", "status": "CONFIRMED - Indiana's first governor", "term": "1816-1822", "historical_significance": "Led Indiana to statehood in 1816" }, "highway_research": { "target": "23.6-mile section of Interstate 65 named after Jonathan Jennings", "search_results_summary": { "total_searches": len(search_queries), "total_results": len(all_search_results), "relevant_results": len(highway_findings['relevant_results']), "legislative_references": len(highway_findings['legislative_references']) }, "findings": highway_findings, "research_status": "IN PROGRESS - Requires additional targeted searches" }, "next_steps": [ "Search for specific Indiana Department of Transportation records", "Look for Indiana General Assembly resolution records", "Search for highway dedication ceremonies or announcements", "Check Indiana historical society records", "Search for news articles about highway naming" ] } # Save comprehensive analysis analysis_file = "workspace/jennings_i65_comprehensive_analysis.json" with open(analysis_file, 'w') as f: json.dump({ "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(), "indiana_governor_data": indiana_governor_data, "comprehensive_analysis": comprehensive_analysis }, f, indent=2) print(f"Comprehensive analysis saved to {analysis_file}") print("\n" + "="*80) print("RESEARCH PROGRESS SUMMARY") print("="*80) print("\n✓ COMPLETED: Governor Identification") print(f"Indiana's first governor: {indiana_governor_data['first_governor']['name']}") print(f"Term of office: {indiana_governor_data['first_governor']['term']}") print(f"Historical significance: {indiana_governor_data['first_governor']['significance']}") print("\n⚠️ IN PROGRESS: I-65 Highway Section Research") print(f"Target: 23.6-mile section of Interstate 65 named after Jonathan Jennings") print(f"Search results analyzed: {len(all_search_results)}") print(f"Relevant findings: {len(highway_findings['relevant_results'])}") if highway_findings['potential_dates']: unique_dates = sorted(set(highway_findings['potential_dates'])) print(f"Potential years mentioned: {', '.join(unique_dates)}") print("\n📋 NEXT RESEARCH PHASE NEEDED:") print("Focus on finding the specific legislative resolution date") print("Key search targets:") for step in comprehensive_analysis['next_steps']: print(f"- {step}") print("\n" + "="*80) print("FILES CREATED:") print(f"- {search_results_file} (search data)") print(f"- {analysis_file} (comprehensive analysis)") print("="*80) print("\nPhase 1 research completed. import os import requests import json from datetime import datetime print("Continuing research on Indiana's first governor and I-65 section naming...") # Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist if not os.path.exists('workspace'): os.makedirs('workspace') print("\nStep 1: Checking for existing research files...") # Check what files exist in workspace workspace_files = [] if os.path.exists('workspace'): workspace_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.endswith('.json')] print(f"Found {len(workspace_files)} JSON files in workspace: {workspace_files}") else: print("No workspace directory found") # Inspect existing files if they exist for filename in workspace_files: filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename) print(f"\nInspecting {filename}:") try: with open(filepath, 'r') as f: data = json.load(f) print(f" Keys: {list(data.keys())}") if 'timestamp' in data: print(f" Created: {data['timestamp']}") if 'total_results' in data: print(f" Total results: {data['total_results']}") if 'governor_identified' in data: print(f" Governor identified: {data['governor_identified']}") except Exception as e: print(f" Error reading file: {str(e)}") print("\nStep 2: Confirming Indiana's first governor information...") # Confirmed historical data about Indiana's first governor jonathan_jennings_data = { "name": "Jonathan Jennings", "role": "First Governor of Indiana", "term": "1816-1822", "birth_year": 1784, "death_year": 1834, "birthplace": "Hunterdon County, New Jersey", "key_facts": [ "Moved to Indiana Territory in 1806", "Served as Indiana's delegate to Congress (1809-1816)", "Instrumental in Indiana achieving statehood on December 11, 1816", "Elected as Indiana's first governor in 1816", "Served two terms as governor (1816-1822)", "Later served in U.S. House of Representatives (1822-1831)", "Died in 1834 in Charlestown, Indiana" ], "significance": "Led Indiana from territory to statehood and served as first chief executive" } print(f"✓ Confirmed: {jonathan_jennings_data['name']} was Indiana's first governor") print(f"✓ Term: {jonathan_jennings_data['term']}") print(f"✓ Key role: {jonathan_jennings_data['significance']}") print("\nStep 3: Focused search for I-65 Jonathan Jennings section and legislative resolution...") # Check for API key api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key: print("SerpAPI key available - conducting targeted searches...") else: print("No SerpAPI key - will use alternative research approach") # More specific search queries focused on legislative resolution targeted_search_queries = [ "\"Jonathan Jennings\" \"Interstate 65\" Indiana resolution legislature", "I-65 Indiana \"Jonathan Jennings\" 23.6 miles named section", "Indiana General Assembly resolution Interstate 65 Jonathan Jennings", "\"Jonathan Jennings Memorial Highway\" I-65 Indiana legislature", "Interstate 65 Indiana governor named section resolution date", "Indiana highway naming Jonathan Jennings I-65 legislative action" ] all_search_results = [] search_summary = { "queries_attempted": 0, "successful_searches": 0, "total_results": 0, "errors": [] } # Perform targeted searches if api_key: for i, query in enumerate(targeted_search_queries, 1): try: print(f"\nSearch {i}/{len(targeted_search_queries)}: {query}") search_summary["queries_attempted"] += 1 params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "num": 8, "safe": "off" } response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=25) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): search_results = results["organic_results"] all_search_results.extend(search_results) search_summary["successful_searches"] += 1 search_summary["total_results"] += len(search_results) print(f" ✓ Found {len(search_results)} results") # Show first result for immediate feedback if search_results: first_result = search_results[0] print(f" Top result: {first_result.get('title', 'No title')}") snippet = first_result.get('snippet', '') if len(snippet) > 100: snippet = snippet[:100] + "..." print(f" Snippet: {snippet}") else: print(" No results found") else: error_msg = f"Search failed with status {response.status_code}" print(f" ✗ {error_msg}") search_summary["errors"].append(error_msg) except Exception as e: error_msg = f"Search error: {str(e)}" print(f" ✗ {error_msg}") search_summary["errors"].append(error_msg) # Delay between searches import time time.sleep(1.5) print(f"\nSearch Summary:") print(f" Queries attempted: {search_summary['queries_attempted']}") print(f" Successful searches: {search_summary['successful_searches']}") print(f" Total results collected: {search_summary['total_results']}") print(f" Errors encountered: {len(search_summary['errors'])}") else: print("Skipping web searches - no API key available") print("\nStep 4: Analyzing search results for legislative resolution information...") # Analyze results for specific information about the resolution legislative_findings = { "resolution_references": [], "highway_naming_info": [], "date_mentions": [], "relevant_links": [], "key_phrases_found": [] } # Keywords to look for legislative_keywords = ['resolution', 'legislature', 'general assembly', 'passed', 'designated', 'named', 'memorial'] highway_keywords = ['interstate 65', 'i-65', '23.6', 'mile', 'section', 'highway', 'jennings'] date_keywords = ['2019', '2020', '2021', '2022', '2023', '2024'] for result in all_search_results: title = result.get('title', '').lower() snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower() link = result.get('link', '') combined_text = title + ' ' + snippet # Check for legislative terms legislative_matches = [kw for kw in legislative_keywords if kw in combined_text] highway_matches = [kw for kw in highway_keywords if kw in combined_text] date_matches = [kw for kw in date_keywords if kw in combined_text] # Score relevance relevance_score = len(legislative_matches) + len(highway_matches) + len(date_matches) if relevance_score >= 3: # High relevance threshold finding = { 'title': result.get('title', ''), 'snippet': result.get('snippet', ''), 'link': link, 'legislative_terms': legislative_matches, 'highway_terms': highway_matches, 'date_terms': date_matches, 'relevance_score': relevance_score } if legislative_matches: legislative_findings['resolution_references'].append(finding) if highway_matches: legislative_findings['highway_naming_info'].append(finding) if date_matches: legislative_findings['date_mentions'].append(finding) legislative_findings['relevant_links'].append(link) # Extract key phrases import re # Look for phrases like "passed resolution", "named section", etc. key_phrases = re.findall(r'\b(?:passed|adopted|designated|named|resolution|memorial)\s+\w+\b', combined_text) legislative_findings['key_phrases_found'].extend(key_phrases) # Remove duplicates and sort legislative_findings['relevant_links'] = list(set(legislative_findings['relevant_links'])) legislative_findings['key_phrases_found'] = list(set(legislative_findings['key_phrases_found'])) print(f"Analysis Results:") print(f" Resolution references: {len(legislative_findings['resolution_references'])}") print(f" Highway naming info: {len(legislative_findings['highway_naming_info'])}") print(f" Date mentions: {len(legislative_findings['date_mentions'])}") print(f" Relevant links: {len(legislative_findings['relevant_links'])}") print(f" Key phrases found: {len(legislative_findings['key_phrases_found'])}") # Display most relevant findings if legislative_findings['resolution_references']: print("\n🏛️ TOP LEGISLATIVE REFERENCES:") # Sort by relevance score sorted_refs = sorted(legislative_findings['resolution_references'], key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True) for i, ref in enumerate(sorted_refs[:3], 1): print(f"\n--- Reference {i} (Score: {ref['relevance_score']}) ---") print(f"Title: {ref['title']}") print(f"Snippet: {ref['snippet']}") print(f"Legislative terms: {', '.join(ref['legislative_terms'])}") print(f"Highway terms: {', '.join(ref['highway_terms'])}") if ref['date_terms']: print(f"Date terms: {', '.join(ref['date_terms'])}") print(f"Link: {ref['link']}") if legislative_findings['key_phrases_found']: print(f"\n🔍 KEY PHRASES DETECTED: {', '.join(legislative_findings['key_phrases_found'][:10])}") print("\nStep 5: Saving comprehensive research results...") # Create final comprehensive report final_report = { "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(), "research_question": "When did Indiana legislature pass resolution to name 23.6-mile I-65 section after Jonathan Jennings?", "governor_confirmed": { "name": jonathan_jennings_data["name"], "term": jonathan_jennings_data["term"], "status": "CONFIRMED - Indiana's first governor" }, "search_execution": search_summary, "legislative_analysis": legislative_findings, "research_status": { "governor_identification": "COMPLETE", "highway_section_research": "IN PROGRESS" if legislative_findings['resolution_references'] else "NEEDS MORE RESEARCH", "resolution_date_found": len(legislative_findings['date_mentions']) > 0 } } # Save final report final_report_file = "workspace/jennings_i65_final_research_report.json" with open(final_report_file, 'w') as f: json.dump(final_report, f, indent=2) # Save detailed search results detailed_results_file = "workspace/jennings_i65_detailed_search_results.json" with open(detailed_results_file, 'w') as f: json.dump({ "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(), "search_queries": targeted_search_queries, "all_results": all_search_results, "analysis": legislative_findings }, f, indent=2) print(f"\n📁 Files saved:") print(f" - {final_report_file}") print(f" - {detailed_results_file}") print("\n" + "="*80) print("FINAL RESEARCH SUMMARY") print("="*80) print(f"\n✅ GOVERNOR IDENTIFIED: {jonathan_jennings_data['name']}") print(f" Role: Indiana's first governor ({jonathan_jennings_data['term']})") print(f" Significance: {jonathan_jennings_data['significance']}") print(f"\n🛣️ I-65 HIGHWAY SECTION RESEARCH:") print(f" Target: 23.6-mile section of Interstate 65 named after Jonathan Jennings") print(f" Search queries executed: {search_summary.get('queries_attempted', 0)}") print(f" Total results analyzed: {search_summary.get('total_results', 0)}") print(f" Legislative references found: {len(legislative_findings.get('resolution_references', []))}") if legislative_findings.get('resolution_references'): print(f"\n🎯 MOST PROMISING LEADS:") top_refs = sorted(legislative_findings['resolution_references'], key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True)[:2] for i, ref in enumerate(top_refs, 1): print(f" {i}. {ref['title']}") if ref['date_terms']: print(f" Potential dates: {', '.join(ref['date_terms'])}") else: print(f"\n⚠️ No definitive legislative resolution information found in current search") print(f" Recommendation: May need more specific searches or different sources") print(f"\n📊 RESEARCH STATUS:") for key, status in final_report['research_status'].items(): print(f" {key.replace('_', ' ').title()}: {status}") print("\n" + "="*80) print("Research phase completed. import os import requests import json from datetime import datetime print("Continuing research on Indiana's first governor and I-65 section naming...") # Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist if not os.path.exists('workspace'): os.makedirs('workspace') print("\nStep 1: Checking for existing research files...") # Check what files exist in workspace workspace_files = [] if os.path.exists('workspace'): workspace_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.endswith('.json')] print(f"Found {len(workspace_files)} JSON files in workspace: {workspace_files}") else: print("No workspace directory found") # Inspect existing files if they exist for filename in workspace_files: filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename) print(f"\nInspecting {filename}:") try: with open(filepath, 'r') as f: data = json.load(f) print(f" Keys: {list(data.keys())}") if 'timestamp' in data: print(f" Created: {data['timestamp']}") if 'total_results' in data: print(f" Total results: {data['total_results']}") if 'governor_identified' in data: print(f" Governor identified: {data['governor_identified']}") except Exception as e: print(f" Error reading file: {str(e)}") print("\nStep 2: Confirming Indiana's first governor information...") # Confirmed historical data about Indiana's first governor jonathan_jennings_data = { "name": "Jonathan Jennings", "role": "First Governor of Indiana", "term": "1816-1822", "birth_year": 1784, "death_year": 1834, "birthplace": "Hunterdon County, New Jersey", "key_facts": [ "Moved to Indiana Territory in 1806", "Served as Indiana's delegate to Congress (1809-1816)", "Instrumental in Indiana achieving statehood on December 11, 1816", "Elected as Indiana's first governor in 1816", "Served two terms as governor (1816-1822)", "Later served in U.S. House of Representatives (1822-1831)", "Died in 1834 in Charlestown, Indiana" ], "significance": "Led Indiana from territory to statehood and served as first chief executive" } print(f"✓ Confirmed: {jonathan_jennings_data['name']} was Indiana's first governor") print(f"✓ Term: {jonathan_jennings_data['term']}") print(f"✓ Key role: {jonathan_jennings_data['significance']}") print("\nStep 3: Focused search for I-65 Jonathan Jennings section and legislative resolution...") # Check for API key api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key: print("SerpAPI key available - conducting targeted searches...") else: print("No SerpAPI key - will use alternative research approach") # More specific search queries focused on legislative resolution targeted_search_queries = [ "\"Jonathan Jennings\" \"Interstate 65\" Indiana resolution legislature", "I-65 Indiana \"Jonathan Jennings\" 23.6 miles named section", "Indiana General Assembly resolution Interstate 65 Jonathan Jennings", "\"Jonathan Jennings Memorial Highway\" I-65 Indiana legislature", "Interstate 65 Indiana governor named section resolution date", "Indiana highway naming Jonathan Jennings I-65 legislative action" ] all_search_results = [] search_summary = { "queries_attempted": 0, "successful_searches": 0, "total_results": 0, "errors": [] } # Perform targeted searches if api_key: for i, query in enumerate(targeted_search_queries, 1): try: print(f"\nSearch {i}/{len(targeted_search_queries)}: {query}") search_summary["queries_attempted"] += 1 params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "num": 8, "safe": "off" } response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=25) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): search_results = results["organic_results"] all_search_results.extend(search_results) search_summary["successful_searches"] += 1 search_summary["total_results"] += len(search_results) print(f" ✓ Found {len(search_results)} results") # Show first result for immediate feedback if search_results: first_result = search_results[0] print(f" Top result: {first_result.get('title', 'No title')}") snippet = first_result.get('snippet', '') if len(snippet) > 100: snippet = snippet[:100] + "..." print(f" Snippet: {snippet}") else: print(" No results found") else: error_msg = f"Search failed with status {response.status_code}" print(f" ✗ {error_msg}") search_summary["errors"].append(error_msg) except Exception as e: error_msg = f"Search error: {str(e)}" print(f" ✗ {error_msg}") search_summary["errors"].append(error_msg) # Delay between searches import time time.sleep(1.5) print(f"\nSearch Summary:") print(f" Queries attempted: {search_summary['queries_attempted']}") print(f" Successful searches: {search_summary['successful_searches']}") print(f" Total results collected: {search_summary['total_results']}") print(f" Errors encountered: {len(search_summary['errors'])}") else: print("Skipping web searches - no API key available") print("\nStep 4: Analyzing search results for legislative resolution information...") # Analyze results for specific information about the resolution legislative_findings = { "resolution_references": [], "highway_naming_info": [], "date_mentions": [], "relevant_links": [], "key_phrases_found": [] } # Keywords to look for legislative_keywords = ['resolution', 'legislature', 'general assembly', 'passed', 'designated', 'named', 'memorial'] highway_keywords = ['interstate 65', 'i-65', '23.6', 'mile', 'section', 'highway', 'jennings'] date_keywords = ['2019', '2020', '2021', '2022', '2023', '2024'] for result in all_search_results: title = result.get('title', '').lower() snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower() link = result.get('link', '') combined_text = title + ' ' + snippet # Check for legislative terms legislative_matches = [kw for kw in legislative_keywords if kw in combined_text] highway_matches = [kw for kw in highway_keywords if kw in combined_text] date_matches = [kw for kw in date_keywords if kw in combined_text] # Score relevance relevance_score = len(legislative_matches) + len(highway_matches) + len(date_matches) if relevance_score >= 3: # High relevance threshold finding = { 'title': result.get('title', ''), 'snippet': result.get('snippet', ''), 'link': link, 'legislative_terms': legislative_matches, 'highway_terms': highway_matches, 'date_terms': date_matches, 'relevance_score': relevance_score } if legislative_matches: legislative_findings['resolution_references'].append(finding) if highway_matches: legislative_findings['highway_naming_info'].append(finding) if date_matches: legislative_findings['date_mentions'].append(finding) legislative_findings['relevant_links'].append(link) # Extract key phrases import re # Look for phrases like "passed resolution", "named section", etc. key_phrases = re.findall(r'\b(?:passed|adopted|designated|named|resolution|memorial)\s+\w+\b', combined_text) legislative_findings['key_phrases_found'].extend(key_phrases) # Remove duplicates and sort legislative_findings['relevant_links'] = list(set(legislative_findings['relevant_links'])) legislative_findings['key_phrases_found'] = list(set(legislative_findings['key_phrases_found'])) print(f"Analysis Results:") print(f" Resolution references: {len(legislative_findings['resolution_references'])}") print(f" Highway naming info: {len(legislative_findings['highway_naming_info'])}") print(f" Date mentions: {len(legislative_findings['date_mentions'])}") print(f" Relevant links: {len(legislative_findings['relevant_links'])}") print(f" Key phrases found: {len(legislative_findings['key_phrases_found'])}") # Display most relevant findings if legislative_findings['resolution_references']: print("\n🏛️ TOP LEGISLATIVE REFERENCES:") # Sort by relevance score sorted_refs = sorted(legislative_findings['resolution_references'], key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True) for i, ref in enumerate(sorted_refs[:3], 1): print(f"\n--- Reference {i} (Score: {ref['relevance_score']}) ---") print(f"Title: {ref['title']}") print(f"Snippet: {ref['snippet']}") print(f"Legislative terms: {', '.join(ref['legislative_terms'])}") print(f"Highway terms: {', '.join(ref['highway_terms'])}") if ref['date_terms']: print(f"Date terms: {', '.join(ref['date_terms'])}") print(f"Link: {ref['link']}") if legislative_findings['key_phrases_found']: print(f"\n🔍 KEY PHRASES DETECTED: {', '.join(legislative_findings['key_phrases_found'][:10])}") print("\nStep 5: Saving comprehensive research results...") # Create final comprehensive report final_report = { "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(), "research_question": "When did Indiana legislature pass resolution to name 23.6-mile I-65 section after Jonathan Jennings?", "governor_confirmed": { "name": jonathan_jennings_data["name"], "term": jonathan_jennings_data["term"], "status": "CONFIRMED - Indiana's first governor" }, "search_execution": search_summary, "legislative_analysis": legislative_findings, "research_status": { "governor_identification": "COMPLETE", "highway_section_research": "IN PROGRESS" if legislative_findings['resolution_references'] else "NEEDS MORE RESEARCH", "resolution_date_found": len(legislative_findings['date_mentions']) > 0 } } # Save final report final_report_file = "workspace/jennings_i65_final_research_report.json" with open(final_report_file, 'w') as f: json.dump(final_report, f, indent=2) # Save detailed search results detailed_results_file = "workspace/jennings_i65_detailed_search_results.json" with open(detailed_results_file, 'w') as f: json.dump({ "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(), "search_queries": targeted_search_queries, "all_results": all_search_results, "analysis": legislative_findings }, f, indent=2) print(f"\n📁 Files saved:") print(f" - {final_report_file}") print(f" - {detailed_results_file}") print("\n" + "="*80) print("FINAL RESEARCH SUMMARY") print("="*80) print(f"\n✅ GOVERNOR IDENTIFIED: {jonathan_jennings_data['name']}") print(f" Role: Indiana's first governor ({jonathan_jennings_data['term']})") print(f" Significance: {jonathan_jennings_data['significance']}") print(f"\n🛣️ I-65 HIGHWAY SECTION RESEARCH:") print(f" Target: 23.6-mile section of Interstate 65 named after Jonathan Jennings") print(f" Search queries executed: {search_summary.get('queries_attempted', 0)}") print(f" Total results analyzed: {search_summary.get('total_results', 0)}") print(f" Legislative references found: {len(legislative_findings.get('resolution_references', []))}") if legislative_findings.get('resolution_references'): print(f"\n🎯 MOST PROMISING LEADS:") top_refs = sorted(legislative_findings['resolution_references'], key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True)[:2] for i, ref in enumerate(top_refs, 1): print(f" {i}. {ref['title']}") if ref['date_terms']: print(f" Potential dates: {', '.join(ref['date_terms'])}") else: print(f"\n⚠️ No definitive legislative resolution information found in current search") print(f" Recommendation: May need more specific searches or different sources") print(f"\n📊 RESEARCH STATUS:") for key, status in final_report['research_status'].items(): print(f" {key.replace('_', ' ').title()}: {status}") print("\n" + "="*80) print("Research phase completed. Results saved to workspace files.") print("="*80)

### Development Step 1: Search and Compile Comprehensive List of Washington State County Seats and Their Counties

**Description**: Search for and compile a comprehensive list of all county seats in Washington state along with their respective counties. Use authoritative government sources such as the Washington State government website, U.S. Census Bureau resources, or reliable reference materials to ensure accuracy and completeness of the county seat information.

**Use Cases**:
- A regional logistics company automating delivery route optimization by using county seat locations as central hubs for multi-stop daily shipments.
- A political campaign team scheduling candidate visits and public events in each county’s seat to ensure comprehensive voter outreach across Washington.
- A GIS software developer integrating county seat coordinates into an emergency response mapping tool for faster dispatch and resource allocation during natural disasters.
- A state tourism board building a mobile app that highlights historical sites, museums, and annual festivals in every Washington county seat.
- A market research analyst segmenting consumer data by county seat to design hyper-local advertising campaigns for retail chains.
- A public health department mapping vaccination clinic coverage relative to each county seat’s population center to identify underserved areas.
- A news organization automating the creation of county-by-county fact sheets for an election guide, including demographics and administrative contacts for each county seat.
- A real estate platform enhancing property search filters by distance to county seat government offices and public amenities for prospective homebuyers.

```
import os
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import json
import time
import re

# Ensure workspace directory exists
workspace = 'workspace'
os.makedirs(workspace, exist_ok=True)

# Initialize results list
results = []

# First, try to get county information from Washington State government sources
print("Step 1: Fetching Washington State county information...")

# Try the Washington State Association of Counties website
wsac_url = 'https://www.wsac.org/counties'
print(f"Fetching: {wsac_url}")

try:
response = requests.get(wsac_url, timeout=15)
response.raise_for_status()
wsac_html = response.text

# Save the HTML for inspection
wsac_html_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'wsac_counties.html')
with open(wsac_html_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(wsac_html)
print(f"Saved WSAC HTML to {wsac_html_path}")

# Parse the HTML
soup = BeautifulSoup(wsac_html, 'html.parser')

# Look for county information - this will vary based on the site structure
# Let's examine the page structure first
print("\nExamining WSAC page structure...")

# Look for common patterns that might contain county information
county_links = soup.find_all('a', href=True)
county_mentions = []

for link in county_links:
link_text = link.get_text(strip=True)
if 'county' in link_text.lower() and len(link_text) < 50:
county_mentions.append({
'text': link_text,
'href': link.get('href')
})

print(f"Found {len(county_mentions)} potential county mentions:")
for mention in county_mentions[:10]: # Show first 10
print(f" - {mention['text']} -> {mention['href']}")

except Exception as e:
print(f"Error fetching WSAC data: {e}")
wsac_html = None

time.sleep(2)

# Try Wikipedia as a reliable backup source
print("\nStep 2: Fetching from Wikipedia...")
wiki_url = 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_counties_in_Washington'
print(f"Fetching: {wiki_url}")

try:
response = requests.get(wiki_url, timeout=15)
response.raise_for_status()
wiki_html = response.text

# Save the HTML
wiki_html_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'wiki_wa_counties.html')
with open(wiki_html_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(wiki_html)
print(f"Saved Wikipedia HTML to {wiki_html_path}")

# Parse Wikipedia page
wiki_soup = BeautifulSoup(wiki_html, 'html.parser')

# Look for the main table with county information
tables = wiki_soup.find_all('table', class_='wikitable')
print(f"Found {len(tables)} wikitable(s)")

if tables:
main_table = tables[0] # Usually the first table contains the county list
rows = main_table.find_all('tr')
print(f"Found {len(rows)} rows in the main table")

# Examine the header to understand the structure
if rows:
header_row = rows[0]
headers = [th.get_text(strip=True) for th in header_row.find_all(['th', 'td'])]
print(f"Table headers: {headers}")

# Process data rows
for i, row in enumerate(rows[1:], 1):
cells = row.find_all(['td', 'th'])
if len(cells) >= 2: # Need at least county name and county seat
county_name = cells[0].get_text(strip=True)
county_seat = cells[1].get_text(strip=True) if len(cells) > 1 else ''

# Clean up the data
county_name = re.sub(r'\[.*?\]', '', county_name).strip()
county_seat = re.sub(r'\[.*?\]', '', county_seat).strip()

if county_name and county_seat:
results.append({
'county': county_name,
'county_seat': county_seat,
'source': 'Wikipedia'
})
print(f" Row {i}: {county_name} -> {county_seat}")

except Exception as e:
print(f"Error fetching Wikipedia data: {e}")

time.sleep(2)

# Try U.S. Census Bureau as another authoritative source
print("\nStep 3: Attempting U.S. Census Bureau source...")
census_url = 'https://www.census.gov/geographies/reference-files/2020/demo/popest/2020-fips.html'
print(f"Fetching: {census_url}")

try:
response = requests.get(census_url, timeout=15)
response.raise_for_status()
census_html = response.text

# Save for inspection
census_html_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'census_fips.html')
with open(census_html_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(census_html)
print(f"Saved Census HTML to {census_html_path}")

except Exception as e:
print(f"Error fetching Census data: {e}")

# Display results summary
print(f"\nStep 4: Results Summary")
print(f"Total county seats found: {len(results)}")

if results:
print("\nFirst 10 entries:")
for i, entry in enumerate(results[:10], 1):
print(f" {i}. {entry['county']} County -> {entry['county_seat']}")

# Save results to JSON
output_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'wa_county_seats.json')
with open(output_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(results, f, indent=2)
print(f"\nSaved {len(results)} county seat records to {output_path}")

# Also create a simple CSV format
csv_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'wa_county_seats.csv')
with open(csv_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write('County,County Seat,Source\n')
for entry in results:
f.write(f"{entry['county']},{entry['county_seat']},{entry['source']}\n")
print(f"Also saved as CSV to {csv_path}")
else:
print("No county seat data was successfully extracted. Will need to try alternative approaches.")

print("\nStep 5: Verification - Washington should have 39 counties")
print(f"We found {len(results)} counties. Expected: 39")
if len(results) != 39:
print("Count mismatch detected - may need to refine extraction or try additional sources")
```

### Development Step 2: Comprehensive List of Washington State County Seats and Corresponding Counties

**Description**: Search for and compile a comprehensive list of all county seats in Washington state along with their respective counties. Use authoritative government sources such as the Washington State government website, U.S. Census Bureau resources, or reliable reference materials to ensure accuracy and completeness of the county seat information.

**Use Cases**:
- Public GIS and mapping portal integration for Washington state government, using the county seat list to dynamically populate county office locations and service boundaries on interactive maps
- Real estate investment analytics that correlate housing market trends with proximity to county seats, providing investors targeted demographic and economic insights per county
- Emergency management dispatch automation that references county seat locations and FIPS codes to optimize resource staging, mutual aid coordination, and evacuation routing during natural disasters
- Travel and tourism itinerary builder app that highlights historic and cultural attractions in each Washington county seat, enabling personalized tour planning and local business recommendations
- E-commerce logistics and tax calculation engine that validates customer addresses against county seats, determines correct tax jurisdictions, and streamlines order fulfillment across Washington counties
- Voter registration and election administration system enhancement that auto-assigns residents to the correct county election office based on county seat data, improving ballot distribution accuracy
- Academic GIS and geography curriculum module for universities, teaching students how to scrape, clean, and visualize spatial data by mapping Washington’s county seats with their FIPS identifiers
- Retail site-selection analysis tool for chain expansion, combining demographic metrics with county seat locations to identify optimal store openings in underserved Washington markets

```
import os
import requests

try:
response = requests.get(wiki_url, timeout=15)
response.raise_for_status()
wiki_html = response.text

# Save the HTML
wiki_html_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'wiki_wa_counties.html')
with open(wiki_html_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(wiki_html)
print(f"Saved Wikipedia HTML to {wiki_html_path}")

# Parse Wikipedia page

# Look for the main table with county information

print(f"Found {len(tables)} wikitable(s)")

if tables:
main_table = tables[0] # Usually the first table contains the county list
rows = main_table.find_all('tr')
print(f"Found {len(rows)} rows in the main table")

# Examine the header to understand the structure
if rows:
header_row = rows[0]
headers = [th.get_text(strip=True) for th in header_row.find_all(['th', 'td'])]
print(f"Table headers: {headers}")
print("\nBased on tester feedback, county seat should be in column index 2 (3rd column)")

# Process data rows - FIX: Use cells[2] for county seat instead of cells[1]
for i, row in enumerate(rows[1:], 1):
cells = row.find_all(['td', 'th'])
if len(cells) >= 3: # Need at least county name, FIPS, and county seat
county_name = cells[0].get_text(strip=True)
fips_code = cells[1].get_text(strip=True) # This was being incorrectly used as county seat
county_seat = cells[2].get_text(strip=True) # CORRECTED: This is the actual county seat

# Clean up the data - remove citation markers
county_name = re.sub(r'\[.*?\]', '', county_name).strip()
county_seat = re.sub(r'\[.*?\]', '', county_seat).strip()

if county_name and county_seat:
results.append({
'county': county_name,
'county_seat': county_seat,
'fips_code': fips_code,
'source': 'Wikipedia'
})
print(f" Row {i}: {county_name} -> {county_seat} (FIPS: {fips_code})")

except Exception as e:
print(f"Error fetching Wikipedia data: {e}")

time.sleep(2)

# Try Washington State Association of Counties as additional verification
print("\nStep 2: Attempting to get additional verification from WSAC...")
wsac_url = 'https://www.wsac.org/counties'
print(f"Fetching: {wsac_url}")

try:
response = requests.get(wsac_url, timeout=15)
response.raise_for_status()
wsac_html = response.text

# Save the HTML for potential manual inspection
wsac_html_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'wsac_counties.html')
with open(wsac_html_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(wsac_html)
print(f"Saved WSAC HTML to {wsac_html_path} for potential manual verification")

except Exception as e:
print(f"Error fetching WSAC data: {e}")

# Display results summary
print(f"\nStep 3: Results Summary")
print(f"Total county seats found: {len(results)}")
print(f"Expected for Washington State: 39 counties")

if results:
print("\nAll Washington State Counties and County Seats:")
for i, entry in enumerate(results, 1):
print(f" {i:2d}. {entry['county']:20s} -> {entry['county_seat']}")

# Save results to JSON
output_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'wa_county_seats.json')
with open(output_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(results, f, indent=2)
print(f"\nSaved {len(results)} county seat records to {output_path}")

# Also create a simple CSV format
csv_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'wa_county_seats.csv')
with open(csv_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write('County,County Seat,FIPS Code,Source\n')
for entry in results:
f.write(f"\"{entry['county']}\",\"{entry['county_seat']}\",{entry['fips_code']},{entry['source']}\n")
print(f"Also saved as CSV to {csv_path}")

# Verification check
if len(results) == 39:
print("\n✓ SUCCESS: Found exactly 39 counties as expected for Washington State")
else:
print(f"\n⚠ WARNING: Found {len(results)} counties, expected 39. May need further verification.")

# Show some sample entries to verify data quality
print("\nSample entries for quality verification:")
sample_entries = [results[0], results[len(results)//2], results[-1]] if len(results) >= 3 else results
for entry in sample_entries:
print(f" {entry['county']} County seat: {entry['county_seat']}")

else:
print("No county seat data was successfully extracted. Will need to try alternative approaches.")

print("\nStep 4: Data source verification")
print("Primary source: Wikipedia List of counties in Washington")
print("This is considered a reliable source for basic geographic and administrative information")
print("Data includes official county names, county seats, and FIPS codes for reference")

### Development Step 5: Compile Official Land Area Measurements for Washington’s 39 County Seats

**Description**: Research and extract the land area data for all 39 Washington state county seats that were identified in the previous step. Use authoritative sources such as the U.S. Census Bureau, official city websites, or government geographic databases to obtain the land area measurements for each county seat city. Focus on finding the official land area figures in square miles or square kilometers for accurate comparison.

**Use Cases**:
- Urban infrastructure planning in Washington state county seats, using precise land area data to design municipal water supply networks and street maintenance schedules
- Public health service optimization across Washington county seats, mapping clinic and vaccination center coverage by city square miles for equitable access
- Emergency management resource allocation for Washington county seats, leveraging land area measurements to position fire stations and disaster response teams efficiently
- Real estate investment analysis targeting Washington county seats, correlating land area figures with property values to identify growth opportunities
- Environmental impact assessments in Washington county seats, calculating per capita green space and planning urban park development based on city land area
- Transportation network design for Washington county seats, using area statistics to model bus routes, bike lanes, and traffic flow projections
- Retail site selection and market entry strategy for chains expanding into Washington county seats, comparing city land area and population density for optimal store placement
- Educational district boundary planning in Washington county seats, utilizing land area data to balance school catchment zones and capacity planning

else:

import os import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import json import time import re # Ensure workspace directory exists workspace = 'workspace' os.makedirs(workspace, exist_ok=True) print("=== RESEARCHING CLARK COUNTY, INDIANA ESTABLISHMENT ===\n") print("Objective: Verify that Clark County, Indiana was established by Virginia colonial legislature in 1783") print("Cross-reference with Interstate 65 Governor Jonathan Jennings Memorial Highway findings\n") # Initialize research results research_results = { 'clark_county_establishment': {}, 'virginia_connection': {}, 'i65_highway_verification': {}, 'sources': [] } # Step 1: Research Clark County, Indiana establishment history print("=== STEP 1: RESEARCHING CLARK COUNTY ESTABLISHMENT HISTORY ===\n") # Try Wikipedia first for Clark County, Indiana wiki_clark_url = 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Clark_County,_Indiana' print(f"Fetching Clark County, Indiana Wikipedia page: {wiki_clark_url}") try: response = requests.get(wiki_clark_url, timeout=15) response.raise_for_status() clark_html = response.text # Save the HTML for inspection clark_html_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'clark_county_indiana_wiki.html') with open(clark_html_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(clark_html) print(f"Saved Clark County Wikipedia HTML to {clark_html_path}") # Parse the HTML soup = BeautifulSoup(clark_html, 'html.parser') # Look for establishment/history information print("\nSearching for establishment date and Virginia connection...") # Search for text containing establishment information page_text = soup.get_text().lower() # Look for key phrases establishment_keywords = ['established', 'founded', 'created', '1783', 'virginia', 'colonial'] relevant_paragraphs = [] # Find paragraphs containing establishment information paragraphs = soup.find_all('p') for para in paragraphs: para_text = para.get_text().lower() if any(keyword in para_text for keyword in establishment_keywords): relevant_paragraphs.append(para.get_text().strip()) print(f"Found {len(relevant_paragraphs)} relevant paragraphs about establishment:") for i, para in enumerate(relevant_paragraphs, 1): print(f"\nParagraph {i}:") print(f"{para[:500]}..." if len(para) > 500 else para) # Look specifically for infobox or history section infobox = soup.find('table', class_='infobox') if infobox: print("\nFound infobox - searching for establishment date...") infobox_text = infobox.get_text() print(f"Infobox content (first 1000 chars): {infobox_text[:1000]}") # Look for establishment date in infobox if '1783' in infobox_text: print("✓ Found 1783 in infobox!") research_results['clark_county_establishment']['found_1783'] = True if 'virginia' in infobox_text.lower(): print("✓ Found Virginia reference in infobox!") research_results['virginia_connection']['found_in_infobox'] = True # Store findings research_results['clark_county_establishment']['wikipedia_paragraphs'] = relevant_paragraphs research_results['sources'].append({ 'url': wiki_clark_url, 'type': 'Wikipedia', 'content_saved': clark_html_path }) except Exception as e: print(f"Error fetching Clark County Wikipedia: {e}") research_results['clark_county_establishment']['wikipedia_error'] = str(e) time.sleep(2) # Step 2: Research Virginia's role in Indiana territory print("\n=== STEP 2: RESEARCHING VIRGINIA'S ROLE IN INDIANA TERRITORY ===\n") # Try Wikipedia page for Indiana Territory or Virginia's western claims virginia_claims_url = 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indiana_Territory' print(f"Fetching Indiana Territory Wikipedia page: {virginia_claims_url}") try: response = requests.get(virginia_claims_url, timeout=15) response.raise_for_status() territory_html = response.text # Save the HTML territory_html_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'indiana_territory_wiki.html') with open(territory_html_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(territory_html) print(f"Saved Indiana Territory Wikipedia HTML to {territory_html_path}") # Parse for Virginia connection soup = BeautifulSoup(territory_html, 'html.parser') # Search for Virginia-related content page_text = soup.get_text().lower() virginia_keywords = ['virginia', '1783', 'colonial', 'legislature', 'clark'] virginia_paragraphs = [] paragraphs = soup.find_all('p') for para in paragraphs: para_text = para.get_text().lower() if 'virginia' in para_text and any(keyword in para_text for keyword in ['1783', 'clark', 'colonial']): virginia_paragraphs.append(para.get_text().strip()) print(f"Found {len(virginia_paragraphs)} paragraphs mentioning Virginia and relevant keywords:") for i, para in enumerate(virginia_paragraphs, 1): print(f"\nVirginia Paragraph {i}:") print(f"{para[:400]}..." if len(para) > 400 else para) research_results['virginia_connection']['territory_paragraphs'] = virginia_paragraphs research_results['sources'].append({ 'url': virginia_claims_url, 'type': 'Wikipedia', 'content_saved': territory_html_path }) except Exception as e: print(f"Error fetching Indiana Territory Wikipedia: {e}") research_results['virginia_connection']['territory_error'] = str(e) time.sleep(2) # Step 3: Verify Interstate 65 information print("\n=== STEP 3: VERIFYING INTERSTATE 65 GOVERNOR JENNINGS MEMORIAL HIGHWAY ===\n") # Search for information about the highway designation i65_search_terms = ['interstate 65 clark county indiana', 'governor jonathan jennings memorial highway'] # Try searching for Indiana highway information indiana_highways_url = 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_state_highways_in_Indiana' print(f"Fetching Indiana highways information: {indiana_highways_url}") try: response = requests.get(indiana_highways_url, timeout=15) response.raise_for_status() highways_html = response.text # Save the HTML highways_html_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'indiana_highways_wiki.html') with open(highways_html_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(highways_html) print(f"Saved Indiana highways Wikipedia HTML to {highways_html_path}") # Search for Jennings Memorial Highway soup = BeautifulSoup(highways_html, 'html.parser') page_text = soup.get_text().lower() jennings_found = 'jennings' in page_text i65_found = 'interstate 65' in page_text or 'i-65' in page_text clark_found = 'clark' in page_text print(f"Search results in Indiana highways page:") print(f" - 'Jennings' found: {jennings_found}") print(f" - 'Interstate 65' or 'I-65' found: {i65_found}") print(f" - 'Clark' found: {clark_found}") if jennings_found: # Find paragraphs mentioning Jennings jennings_paragraphs = [] paragraphs = soup.find_all('p') for para in paragraphs: para_text = para.get_text() if 'jennings' in para_text.lower(): jennings_paragraphs.append(para_text.strip()) print(f"\nFound {len(jennings_paragraphs)} paragraphs mentioning Jennings:") for i, para in enumerate(jennings_paragraphs, 1): print(f"\nJennings Paragraph {i}:") print(f"{para[:300]}..." if len(para) > 300 else para) research_results['i65_highway_verification']['jennings_paragraphs'] = jennings_paragraphs research_results['i65_highway_verification']['search_results'] = { 'jennings_found': jennings_found, 'i65_found': i65_found, 'clark_found': clark_found } research_results['sources'].append({ 'url': indiana_highways_url, 'type': 'Wikipedia', 'content_saved': highways_html_path }) except Exception as e: print(f"Error fetching Indiana highways information: {e}") research_results['i65_highway_verification']['highways_error'] = str(e) # Step 4: Summary and conclusions print("\n=== STEP 4: RESEARCH SUMMARY AND CONCLUSIONS ===\n") # Save all research results results_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'clark_county_research_results.json') with open(results_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(research_results, f, indent=2) print(f"Saved comprehensive research results to {results_path}") # Analyze findings print("\nFINDINGS ANALYSIS:") print("=" * 50) print("\n1. CLARK COUNTY ESTABLISHMENT:") if 'wikipedia_paragraphs' in research_results['clark_county_establishment']: paras = research_results['clark_county_establishment']['wikipedia_paragraphs'] print(f" - Found {len(paras)} relevant paragraphs about establishment") # Check if any paragraph mentions both 1783 and Virginia virginia_1783_found = False for para in paras: if '1783' in para and 'virginia' in para.lower(): virginia_1783_found = True print(f" ✓ MATCH FOUND: Paragraph contains both '1783' and 'Virginia'") print(f" Excerpt: {para[:200]}...") break if not virginia_1783_found: print(f" ⚠ No paragraph found containing both '1783' and 'Virginia'") else: print(f" ⚠ No establishment paragraphs found") print("\n2. VIRGINIA CONNECTION:") if 'territory_paragraphs' in research_results['virginia_connection']: paras = research_results['virginia_connection']['territory_paragraphs'] print(f" - Found {len(paras)} paragraphs about Virginia's role") for i, para in enumerate(paras, 1): print(f" Para {i}: {para[:150]}...") else: print(f" ⚠ No Virginia connection paragraphs found") print("\n3. INTERSTATE 65 HIGHWAY VERIFICATION:") if 'search_results' in research_results['i65_highway_verification']: results = research_results['i65_highway_verification']['search_results'] print(f" - Jennings found in highways page: {results['jennings_found']}") print(f" - Interstate 65 found: {results['i65_found']}") print(f" - Clark found: {results['clark_found']}") if results['jennings_found']: print(f" ✓ Governor Jennings reference found in Indiana highways information") else: print(f" ⚠ No highway search results available") print("\n4. OVERALL ASSESSMENT:") print(f" Sources consulted: {len(research_results['sources'])}") for i, source in enumerate(research_results['sources'], 1): print(f" {i}. {source['type']}: {source['url']}") print("\n" + "=" * 50) print("RESEARCH COMPLETE - Data saved for further analysis") print(f"All HTML files and research results saved in {workspace}/") print("Next step: Manual review of saved content for definitive verification")

Search for Jennings Memorial Highway soup = BeautifulSoup(highways_html, 'html.parser') page_text = soup.get_text().lower() jennings_found = 'jennings' in page_text i65_found = 'interstate 65' in page_text or 'i-65' in page_text clark_found = 'clark' in page_text print(f"Search results in Indiana highways page:") print(f" - 'Jennings' found: {jennings_found}") print(f" - 'Interstate 65' or 'I-65' found: {i65_found}") print(f" - 'Clark' found: {clark_found}") if jennings_found: # Find paragraphs mentioning Jennings jennings_paragraphs = [] paragraphs = soup.find_all('p') for para in paragraphs: para_text = para.get_text() if 'jennings' in para_text.lower(): jennings_paragraphs.append(para_text.strip()) print(f"\nFound {len(jennings_paragraphs)} paragraphs mentioning Jennings:") for i, para in enumerate(jennings_paragraphs, 1): print(f"\nJennings Paragraph {i}:") print(f"{para[:300]}..." if len(para) > 300 else para) research_results['i65_highway_verification']['jennings_paragraphs'] = jennings_paragraphs research_results['i65_highway_verification']['search_results'] = { 'jennings_found': jennings_found, 'i65_found': i65_found, 'clark_found': clark_found } research_results['sources'].append({ 'url': indiana_highways_url, 'type': 'Wikipedia', 'content_saved': highways_html_path }) except Exception as e: print(f"Error fetching Indiana highways information: {e}") research_results['i65_highway_verification']['highways_error'] = str(e) # Step 4: Summary and conclusions print("\n=== STEP 4: RESEARCH SUMMARY AND CONCLUSIONS ===\n") # Save all research results results_path = os.path.join(workspace, 'clark_county_research_results.json') with open(results_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(research_results, f, indent=2) print(f"Saved comprehensive research results to {results_path}") # Analyze findings print("\nFINDINGS ANALYSIS:") print("=" * 50) print("\n1. CLARK COUNTY ESTABLISHMENT:") if 'wikipedia_paragraphs' in research_results['clark_county_establishment']: paras = research_results['clark_county_establishment']['wikipedia_paragraphs'] print(f" - Found {len(paras)} relevant paragraphs about establishment") # Check if any paragraph mentions both 1783 and Virginia virginia_1783_found = False for para in paras: if '1783' in para and 'virginia' in para.lower(): virginia_1783_found = True print(f" ✓ MATCH FOUND: Paragraph contains both '1783' and 'Virginia'") print(f" Excerpt: {para[:200]}...") break if not virginia_1783_found: print(f" ⚠ No paragraph found containing both '1783' and 'Virginia'") else: print(f" ⚠ No establishment paragraphs found") print("\n2. VIRGINIA CONNECTION:") if 'territory_paragraphs' in research_results['virginia_connection']: paras = research_results['virginia_connection']['territory_paragraphs'] print(f" - Found {len(paras)} paragraphs about Virginia's role") for i, para in enumerate(paras, 1): print(f" Para {i}: {para[:150]}...") else: print(f" ⚠ No Virginia connection paragraphs found") print("\n3. INTERSTATE 65 HIGHWAY VERIFICATION:") if 'search_results' in research_results['i65_highway_verification']: results = research_results['i65_highway_verification']['search_results'] print(f" - Jennings found in highways page: {results['jennings_found']}") print(f" - Interstate 65 found: {results['i65_found']}") print(f" - Clark found: {results['clark_found']}") if results['jennings_found']: print(f" ✓ Governor Jennings reference found in Indiana highways information") else: print(f" ⚠ No highway search results available") print("\n4. OVERALL ASSESSMENT:") print(f" Sources consulted: {len(research_results['sources'])}") for i, source in enumerate(research_results['sources'], 1): print(f" {i}. {source['type']}: {source['url']}") print("\n" + "=" * 50) print("RESEARCH COMPLETE - Data saved for further analysis") print(f"All HTML files and research results saved in {workspace}/") print("Next step: Manual review of saved content for definitive verification")
